<s> [Sidenote: Miss Emily Jolly.] 3, ALBION VILLAS, FOLKESTONE, KENT, _Tuesday, 17th July, 1855._ DEAR MADAM,[62] Your manuscript, entitled a "Wife's Story," has come under my own perusal within these last three or four days </s>
<s> I recognise in it such great merit and unusual promise, and I think it displays so much power and knowledge of the human heart, that I feel a strong interest in you as its writer </s>
<s> I have begged the gentleman, who is in my confidence as to the transaction of the business of "Household Words," to return the MS </s>
<s> to you by the post, which (as I hope) will convey this note to you </s>
<s> My object is this: I particularly entreat you to consider the catastrophe </s>
<s> You write to be read, of course </s>
<s> The close of the story is unnecessarily painful--will throw off numbers of persons who would otherwise read it, and who (as it stands) will be deterred by hearsay from so doing, and is so tremendous a piece of severity, that it will defeat your purpose </s>
<s> All my knowledge and experience, such as they are, lead me straight to the recommendation that you will do well to spare the life of the husband, and of one of the children </s>
<s> Let her suppose the former dead, from seeing him brought in wounded and insensible--lose nothing of the progress of her mental suffering afterwards when that doctor is in attendance upon her--but bring her round at last to the blessed surprise that her husband is still living, and that a repentance which can be worked out, _in the way of atonement for the misery she has occasioned to the man whom she so ill repaid for his love, and made so miserable_, lies before her </s>
<s> So will you soften the reader whom you now as it were harden, and so you will bring tears from many eyes, which can only have their spring in affectionately and gently touched hearts </s>
<s> I am perfectly certain that with this change, all the previous part of your tale will tell for twenty times as much as it can in its present condition </s>
<s> And it is because I believe you have a great fame before you if you do justice to the remarkable ability you possess, that I venture to offer you this advice in what I suppose to be the beginning of your career </s>
<s> I observe some parts of the story which would be strengthened, even in their psychological interest, by condensation here and there </s>
<s> If you will leave that to me, I will perform the task as conscientiously and carefully as if it were my own </s>
<s> But the suggestion I offer for your acceptance, no one but yourself can act upon </s>
<s> Let me conclude this hasty note with the plain assurance that I have never been so much surprised and struck by any manuscript I have read, as I have been by yours </s>
<s> Your faithful Servant </s>
<s> [Sidenote: The same.] 3, ALBION VILLAS, FOLKESTONE, _July 21st, 1855._ DEAR MADAM, I did not enter, in detail, on the spirit of the alteration I propose in your story; because I thought it right that you should think out that for yourself if you applied yourself to the change </s>
<s> I can now assure you that you describe it exactly as I had conceived it; and if I had wanted anything to confirm me in my conviction of its being right, our both seeing it so precisely from the same point of view, would be ample assurance to me </s>

<s> I shall quite understand that, and my interest will keep </s>

<s> Kenny.] TAVISTOCK HOUSE, _Monday, 19th May, 1856._ GENTLEMEN, I have received a letter signed by you (which I assume to be written mainly on behalf of what are called Working-Men and their families) inviting me to attend a meeting in our Parish Vestry Hall this evening on the subject of the stoppage of the Sunday bands in the Parks </s>
<s> I thoroughly agree with you that those bands have afforded an innocent and healthful enjoyment on the Sunday afternoon, to which the people have a right </s>
<s> But I think it essential that the working people should, of themselves and by themselves, assert that right </s>
<s> They have been informed, on the high authority of their first Minister (lately rather in want of House of Commons votes I am told) that they are almost indifferent to it </s>
<s> The correction of that mistake, if official omniscience can be mistaken, lies with themselves </s>
<s> In case it should be considered by the meeting, which I prefer for this reason not to attend, expedient to unite with other Metropolitan parishes in forming a fund for the payment of such expenses as may be incurred in peaceably and numerously representing to the governing powers that the harmless recreation they have taken away is very much wanted, I beg you to put down my name as a subscriber of ten pounds </s>
<s> And I am, your faithful Servant </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr Washington Irving.] TAVISTOCK HOUSE, _London, July 5th, 1856._ MY DEAR IRVING, If you knew how often I write to you individually and personally in my books, you would be no more surprised in seeing this note than you were in seeing me do my duty by that flowery julep (in what I dreamily apprehend to have been a former state of existence) at Baltimore </s>
<s> Will you let me present to you a cousin of mine, Mr B----, who is associated with a merchant's house in New York </s>
<s> Of course he wants to see you, and know you </s>
<s> How can _I_ wonder at that </s>
<s> How can anybody </s>
<s> I had a long talk with Leslie at the last Academy dinner (having previously been with him in Paris), and he told me that you were flourishing </s>
<s> I suppose you know that he wears a moustache--so do I for the matter of that, and a beard too--and that he looks like a portrait of Don Quixote </s>
<s> Holland House has four-and-twenty youthful pages in it now--twelve for my lord, and twelve for my lady; and no clergyman coils his leg up under his chair all dinner-time, and begins to uncurve it when the hostess goes </s>
<s> No wheeled chair runs smoothly in with that beaming face in it; and ----'s little cotton pocket-handkerchief helped to make (I believe) this very sheet of paper </s>
<s> A half-sad, half-ludicrous story of Rogers is all I will sully it with </s>
<s> You know, I daresay, that for a year or so before his death he wandered, and lost himself like one of the Children in the Wood, grown up there and grown down again </s>
<s> He had Mrs Procter and Mrs Carlyle to breakfast with him one morning--only those two </s>
<s> Both excessively talkative, very quick and clever, and bent on entertaining him </s>
<s> When Mrs Carlyle had flashed and shone before him for about three-quarters of an hour on one subject, he turned his poor old eyes on Mrs Procter, and pointing to the brilliant discourser with his poor old finger, said (indignantly), "Who is _she_" </s>
<s> Upon this, Mrs Procter, cutting in, delivered (it is her own story) a neat oration on the life and writings of Carlyle, and enlightened him in her happiest and airiest manner; all of which he heard, staring in the dreariest silence, and then said (indignantly, as before), "And who are _you_" </s>
<s> Ever, my dear Irving, Most affectionately and truly yours </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Sir Edward Bulwer Lytton.] TAVISTOCK HOUSE, _Wednesday, 28th January, 1857._ MY DEAR BULWER, I thought Wills had told you as to the Guild (for I begged him to) that he can do absolutely nothing until our charter is seven years old </s>
<s> It is the stringent and express prohibition of the Act of Parliament--for which things you members, thank God, are responsible and not I </s>
<s> When I observed this clause (which was just as we were going to grant a pension, if we could agree on a good subject), I caused our Counsel's opinion to be taken on it, and there is not a doubt about it </s>
<s> I immediately recommended that there should be no expenses--that the interest on the capital should be all invested as it accrued--that the chambers should be given up and the clerk discharged--and that the Guild should have the use of the "Household Words" office rent free, and the services of Wills on the same terms </s>
<s> All of which was done </s>
<s> A letter is now copying, to be sent round to all the members, explaining, with the New Year, the whole state of the thing </s>
<s> You will receive this </s>
<s> It appears to me that it looks wholesome enough </s>
<s> But if a strong idiot comes and binds your hands, or mine, or both, for seven years, what is to be done against him </s>
<s> As to greater matters than this, however--as to all matters on this teeming Earth--it appears to me that the House of Commons and Parliament altogether, is just the dreariest failure and nuisance that has bothered this much-bothered world </s>
<s> Ever yours </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Emily Jolly.] GRAVESEND, KENT, _10th April, 1857._ DEAR MADAM, As I am away from London for a few days, your letter has been forwarded to me </s>
<s> I can honestly encourage and assure you that I believe the depression and want of confidence under which you describe yourself as labouring to have no sufficient foundation </s>
<s> First as to "Mr Arle" </s>
<s> I have constantly heard it spoken of with great approval, and I think it a book of considerable merit </s>
<s> If I were to tell you that I see no evidence of inexperience in it, that would not be true </s>
<s> I think a little more stir and action to be desired also; but I am surprised by your being despondent about it, for I assure you that I had supposed it (always remembering that it is your first novel) to have met with a very good reception </s>
<s> I can bring to my memory--here, with no means of reference at hand--only two papers of yours that have been unsuccessful at "Household Words" </s>
<s> I think the first was called "The Brook" </s>
<s> It appeared to me to break down upon a confusion that pervaded it, between a Coroner's Inquest and a Trial </s>
<s> I have a general recollection of the mingling of the two, as to facts and forms that should have been kept apart, in some inextricable manner that was beyond my powers of disentanglement </s>
<s> The second was about a wife's writing a Novel and keeping the secret from her husband until it was done </s>
<s> I did not think the incident of sufficient force to justify the length of the narrative </s>
<s> But there is nothing fatal in either of these mischances </s>
<s> Mr Wills told me when I spoke to him of the latter paper that you had it in contemplation to offer a longer story to "Household Words" </s>
<s> If you should do so, I assure you I shall be happy to read it myself, and that I shall have a sincere desire to accept it, if possible </s>
<s> I can give you no better counsel than to look into the life about you, and to strive for what is noblest and true </s>
<s> As to further encouragement, I do not, I can most strongly add, believe that you have any reason to be downhearted </s>
<s> Very faithfully yours </s>
<s> [Sidenote: The same.] TAVISTOCK HOUSE, _Saturday Morning, 30th May, 1857._ DEAR MADAM, I read your story, with all possible attention, last night </s>
<s> I cannot tell you with what reluctance I write to you respecting it, for my opinion of it is _not_ favourable, although I perceive your heart in it, and great strength </s>
<s> Pray understand that I claim no infallibility </s>
<s> I merely express my own honest opinion, formed against my earnest desire </s>
<s> I do not lay it down as law for others, though, of course, I believe that many others would come to the same conclusion </s>
<s> It appears to me that the story is one that cannot possibly be told within the compass to which you have limited yourself </s>
<s> The three principal people are, every one of them, in the wrong with the reader, and you cannot put any of them right, without making the story extend over a longer space of time, and without anatomising the souls of the actors more slowly and carefully </s>
<s> Nothing would justify the departure of Alice, but her having some strong reason to believe that in taking that step, _she saved her lover_ </s>
<s> In your intentions as to that lover's transfer of his affections to Eleanor, I descry a striking truth; but I think it confusedly wrought out, and all but certain to fail in expressing itself </s>
<s> Eleanor, I regard as forced and overstrained </s>
<s> The natural result is, that she carries a train of anti-climax after her </s>
<s> I particularly notice this at the point when she thinks she is going to be drowned </s>
<s> The whole idea of the story is sufficiently difficult to require the most exact truth and the greatest knowledge and skill in the colouring throughout </s>
<s> In this respect I have no doubt of its being extremely defective </s>
<s> The people do not talk as such people would; and the little subtle touches of description which, by making the country house and the general scene real, would give an air of reality to the people (much to be desired) are altogether wanting </s>
<s> The more you set yourself to the illustration of your heroine's passionate nature, the more indispensable this attendant atmosphere of truth becomes </s>
<s> It would, in a manner, oblige the reader to believe in her </s>
<s> Whereas, for ever exploding like a great firework without any background, she glares and wheels and hisses, and goes out, and has lighted nothing </s>
<s> Lastly, I fear she is too convulsive from beginning to end </s>
<s> Pray reconsider, from this point of view, her brow, and her eyes, and her drawing herself up to her full height, and her being a perfumed presence, and her floating into rooms, also her asking people how they dare, and the like, on small provocation </s>
<s> When she hears her music being played, I think she is particularly objectionable </s>
<s> I have a strong belief that if you keep this story by you three or four years, you will form an opinion of it not greatly differing from mine </s>
<s> There is so much good in it, so much reflection, so much passion and earnestness, that, if my judgment be right, I feel sure you will come over to it </s>
<s> On the other hand, I do not think that its publication, as it stands, would do you service, or be agreeable to you hereafter </s>
<s> I have no means of knowing whether you are patient in the pursuit of this art; but I am inclined to think that you are not, and that you do not discipline yourself enough </s>
<s> When one is impelled to write this or that, one has still to consider: "How much of this will tell for what I mean </s>
<s> How much of it is my own wild emotion and superfluous energy--how much remains that is truly belonging to this ideal character and these ideal circumstances" </s>
<s> It is in the laborious struggle to make this distinction, and in the determination to try for it, that the road to the correction of faults lies </s>
<s> [Perhaps I may remark, in support of the sincerity with which I write this, that I am an impatient and impulsive person myself, but that it has been for many years the constant effort of my life to practise at my desk what I preach to you.] I should not have written so much, or so plainly, but for your last letter to me </s>
<s> It seems to demand that I should be strictly true with you, and I am so in this letter, without any reservation either way </s>
<s> Very faithfully yours </s>
<s> 1858 </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr Albert Smith.] TAVISTOCK HOUSE, TAVISTOCK SQUARE, LONDON, W.C., _Wednesday Night, 1st December, 1858._ MY DEAR ALBERT, I cannot tell you how grieved I am for poor dear Arthur (even you can hardly love him better than I do), or with what anxiety I shall wait for further news of him </s>

<s> Ever faithfully </s>

<s> For you must both take notice, please, that I have a reminder of you always before me </s>

<s> The leaves on the oak-trees outside the window are less constant than these, for they are with me through the four seasons </s>
<s> Lord </s>
<s> to think of the bygone day when you were stricken mute (was it not at Glasgow?) and, being mounted on a tall ladder at a practicable window, stared at Forster, and with a noble constancy refused to utter word </s>
<s> Like the Monk among the pictures with Wilkie, I begin to think _that_ the real world, and this the sham that goes out with the lights </s>
<s> God bless you both </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Mr Henry F </s>
<s> Chorley.] [69]TAVISTOCK HOUSE, TAVISTOCK SQUARE, W.C., _Friday Night, Feb </s>
<s> 3, 1860._ MY DEAR CHORLEY, I can most honestly assure you that I think "Roccabella" a very remarkable book indeed </s>
<s> Apart--quite apart--from my interest in you, I am certain that if I had taken it up under any ordinarily favourable circumstances as a book of which I knew nothing whatever, I should not--could not--have relinquished it until I had read it through </s>
<s> I had turned but a few pages, and come to the shadow on the bright sofa at the foot of the bed, when I knew myself to be in the hands of an artist </s>
<s> That rare and delightful recognition I never lost for a moment until I closed the second volume at the end </s>
<s> I am "a good audience" when I have reason to be, and my girls would testify to you, if there were need, that I cried over it heartily </s>
<s> Your story seems to me remarkably ingenious </s>
<s> I had not the least idea of the purport of the sealed paper until you chose to enlighten me; and then I felt it to be quite natural, quite easy, thoroughly in keeping with the character and presentation of the Liverpool man </s>
<s> The position of the Bell family in the story has a special air of nature and truth; is quite new to me, and is so dexterously and delicately done that I find the deaf daughter no less real and distinct than the clergyman's wife </s>
<s> The turn of the story round that damnable Princess I pursued with a pleasure with which I could pursue nothing but a true interest; and I declare to you that if I were put upon finding anything better than the scene of Roccabella's death, I should stare round my bookshelves very much at a loss for a long time </s>
<s> Similarly, your characters have really surprised me </s>
<s> From the lawyer to the Princess, I swear to them as true; and in your fathoming of Rosamond altogether, there is a profound wise knowledge that I admire and respect with a heartiness not easily overstated in words </s>
<s> I am not quite with you as to the Italians </s>
<s> Your knowledge of the Italian character seems to me surprisingly subtle and penetrating; but I think we owe it to those most unhappy men and their political wretchedness to ask ourselves mercifully, whether their faults are not essentially the faults of a people long oppressed and priest-ridden;--whether their tendency to slink and conspire is not a tendency that spies in every dress, from the triple crown to a lousy head, have engendered in their ancestors through generations </s>
<s> Again, like you, I shudder at the distresses that come of these unavailing risings; my blood runs hotter, as yours does, at the thought of the leaders safe, and the instruments perishing by hundreds; yet what is to be done </s>
<s> Their wrongs are so great that they _will_ rise from time to time somehow </s>
<s> It would be to doubt the eternal providence of God to doubt that they will rise successfully at last </s>
<s> Unavailing struggles against a dominant tyranny precede all successful turning against it </s>
<s> And is it not a little hard in us Englishman, whose forefathers have risen so often and striven against so much, to look on, in our own security, through microscopes, and detect the motes in the brains of men driven mad </s>
<s> Think, if you and I were Italians, and had grown from boyhood to our present time, menaced in every day through all these years by that infernal confessional, dungeons, and soldiers, could we be better than these men </s>
<s> Should we be so good </s>
<s> I should not, I am afraid, if I know myself </s>
<s> Such things would make of me a moody, bloodthirsty, implacable man, who would do anything for revenge; and if I compromised the truth--put it at the worst, habitually--where should I ever have had it before me </s>
<s> In the old Jesuits' college at Genoa, on the Chiaja at Naples, in the churches of Rome, at the University of Padua, on the Piazzo San Marco at Venice, where </s>
<s> And the government is in all these places, and in all Italian places </s>
<s> I have seen something of these men </s>
<s> I have known Mazzini and Gallenga; Manin was tutor to my daughters in Paris; I have had long talks about scores of them with poor Ary Scheffer, who was their best friend </s>
<s> I have gone back to Italy after ten years, and found the best men I had known there exiled or in jail </s>
<s> I believe they have the faults you ascribe to them (nationally, not individually), but I could not find it in my heart, remembering their miseries, to exhibit those faults without referring them back to their causes </s>
<s> You will forgive my writing this, because I write it exactly as I write my cordial little tribute to the high merits of your book </s>
<s> If it were not a living reality to me, I should care nothing about this point of disagreement; but you are far too earnest a man, and far too able a man, to be left unremonstrated with by an admiring reader </s>
<s> You cannot write so well without influencing many people </s>
<s> If you could tell me that your book had but twenty readers, I would reply, that so good a book will influence more people's opinions, through those twenty, than a worthless book would through twenty thousand; and I express this with the perfect confidence of one in whose mind the book has taken, for good and all, a separate and distinct place </s>
<s> Accept my thanks for the pleasure you have given me </s>
<s> The poor acknowledgment of testifying to that pleasure wherever I go will be my pleasure in return </s>
<s> And so, my dear Chorley, good night, and God bless you </s>
<s> Ever faithfully yours </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Sir John Bowring.] GAD'S HILL, _Wednesday, 31st October, 1860._ MY DEAR SIR JOHN,[70] First let me congratulate you on your marriage and wish you all happiness and prosperity </s>
<s> Secondly, I must tell you that I was greatly vexed with the Chatham people for not giving me early notice of your lecture </s>
<s> In that case I should (of course) have presided, as President of the Institution, and I should have asked you to honour my Falstaff house here </s>
<s> But when they made your kind intention known to me, I had made some important business engagements at the "All the Year Round" office for that evening, which I could not possibly forego </s>
<s> I charged them to tell you so, and was going to write to you when I found your kind letter </s>
<s> Thanks for your paper, which I have sent to the Printer's with much pleasure </s>
<s> We heard of your accident here, and of your "making nothing of it" </s>
<s> I said that you didn't make much of disasters, and that you took poison (from natives) as quite a matter of course in the way of business </s>
<s> Faithfully yours </s>

<s> Layard.] GAD'S HILL PLACE, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, KENT, _Tuesday, 4th December, 1860._ MY DEAR LAYARD, I know you will readily believe that I would come if I could, and that I am heartily sorry I cannot </s>
<s> A new story of my writing, nine months long, is just begun in "All the Year Round" </s>
<s> A certain allotment of my time when I have that story-demand upon me, has, all through my author life, been an essential condition of my health and success </s>
<s> I have just returned here to work so many hours every day for so many days </s>
<s> It is really impossible for me to break my bond </s>
<s> There is not a man in England who is more earnestly your friend and admirer than I am </s>
<s> The conviction that you know it, helps me out through this note </s>
<s> You are a man of so much mark to me, that I even regret your going into the House of Commons--for which assembly I have but a scant respect </s>
<s> But I would not mention it to the Southwark electors if I could come to-morrow; though I should venture to tell them (and even that your friends would consider very impolitic) that I think them very much honoured by having such a candidate for their suffrages </s>

<s> If they had votes for Southwark they would threaten to oppose you--but would never do it </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Mrs Malleson.] OFFICE OF "ALL THE YEAR ROUND," _Monday, 14th January, 1861._ MY DEAR MRS </s>
<s> MALLESON, I am truly sorry that I cannot have the pleasure of dining with you on Thursday </s>
<s> Although I consider myself quite well, and although my doctor almost admits the fact when I indignantly tax him with it, I am not discharged </s>
<s> His treatment renders him very fearful that I should take cold in going to and fro; and he makes excuses, therefore (as I darkly suspect), for keeping me here until said treatment is done with </s>
<s> This morning he tells me he must see me "once more, on Wednesday" </s>
<s> As he has said the like for a whole week, my confidence is not blooming enough at this present writing to justify me in leaving a possibility of Banquo's place at your table </s>
<s> Hence this note </s>
<s> It is screwed out of me </s>
<s> With kind regards to Mr Malleson, believe me, Ever faithfully yours </s>

<s> [Sidenote: The same.] 3, HANOVER TERRACE, _Sunday, 12th May, 1861._ MY DEAR BULWER LYTTON, I received your revised proofs only yesterday, and I sat down to read them last night </s>
<s> And before I say anything further I may tell you that I COULD NOT lay them aside, but was obliged to go on with them in my bedroom until I got into a very ghostly state indeed </s>
<s> This morning I have taken them again and have gone through them with the utmost attention </s>
<s> Of the beauty and power of the writing I say not a word, or of its originality and boldness, or of its quite extraordinary constructive skill </s>
<s> I confine myself solely to your misgiving, and to the question whether there is any sufficient foundation for it </s>
<s> On the last head I say, without the faintest hesitation, most decidedly there is NOT sufficient foundation for it </s>
<s> I do not share it in the least </s>
<s> I believe that the readers who have here given their minds (or perhaps had any to give) to those strange psychological mysteries in ourselves, of which we are all more or less conscious, will accept your wonders as curious weapons in the armoury of fiction, and will submit themselves to the Art with which said weapons are used </s>
<s> Even to that class of intelligence the marvellous addresses itself from a very strong position; and that class of intelligence is not accustomed to find the marvellous in such very powerful hands as yours </s>
<s> On more imaginative readers the tale will fall (or I am greatly mistaken) like a spell </s>
<s> By readers who combine some imagination, some scepticism, and some knowledge and learning, I hope it will be regarded as full of strange fancy and curious study, startling reflections of their own thoughts and speculations at odd times, and wonder which a master has a right to evoke </s>
<s> In the last point lies, to my thinking, the whole case </s>
<s> If you were the Magician's servant instead of the Magician, these potent spirits would get the better of you; but you _are_ the Magician, and they don't, and you make them serve your purpose </s>
<s> Occasionally in the dialogue I see an expression here and there which might--always solely with a reference to your misgiving--be better away; and I think that the vision, to use the word for want of a better--in the museum, should be made a little less abstruse </s>
<s> I should not say that, if the sale of the journal was below the sale of _The Times_ newspaper; but as it is probably several thousands higher, I do </s>
<s> I would also suggest that after the title we put the two words--A ROMANCE </s>
<s> It is an absurdly easy device for getting over your misgiving with the blockheads, but I think it would be an effective one </s>
<s> I don't, on looking at it, like the title </s>
<s> Here are a few that have occurred to me </s>
<s> "The Steel Casket" </s>
<s> "The Lost Manuscript" </s>
<s> "Derval Court" </s>
<s> "Perpetual Youth" </s>
<s> "Maggie" </s>
<s> "Dr </s>
<s> Fenwick" </s>
<s> "Life and Death" </s>
<s> The four last I think the best </s>
<s> There is an objection to "Dr </s>
<s> Fenwick" because there has been "Dr </s>
<s> Antonio," and there is a book of Dumas' which repeats the objection </s>
<s> I don't think "Fenwick" startling enough </s>
<s> It appears to me that a more startling title would take the (John) Bull by the horns, and would be a serviceable concession to your misgiving, as suggesting a story off the stones of the gas-lighted Brentford Road </s>
<s> The title is the first thing to be settled, and cannot be settled too soon </s>
<s> For the purposes of the weekly publication the divisions of the story will often have to be greatly changed, though afterwards, in the complete book, you can, of course, divide it into chapters, free from that reference </s>
<s> For example: I would end the first chapter on the third slip at "and through the ghostly streets, under the ghostly moon, went back to my solitary room" </s>
<s> The rest of what is now your first chapter might be made Chapter II., and would end the first weekly part </s>
<s> I think I have become, by dint of necessity and practice, rather cunning in this regard; and perhaps you would not mind my looking closely to such points from week to week </s>
<s> It so happens that if you had written the opening of this story expressly for the occasion its striking incidents could not possibly have followed one another better </s>
<s> One other merely mechanical change I suggest now </s>
<s> I would not have an initial letter for the town, but would state in the beginning that I gave the town a fictitious name </s>
<s> I suppose a blank or a dash rather fends a good many people off--because it always has that effect upon me </s>
<s> Be sure that I am perfectly frank and open in all I have said in this note, and that I have not a grain of reservation in my mind </s>
<s> I think the story a very fine one, one that no other man could write, and that there is no strength in your misgiving for the two reasons: firstly, that the work is professedly a work of Fancy and Fiction, in which the reader is not required against his will to take everything for Fact; secondly, that it is written by the man who can write it </s>
<s> The Magician's servant does not know what to do with the ghost, and has, consequently, no business with him </s>
<s> The Magician does know what to do with him, and has all the business with him that he can transact </s>
<s> I am quite at ease on the points that you have expressed yourself as not at ease upon </s>
<s> Quite </s>
<s> I cannot too often say that if they were carried on weak shoulders they would break the bearer down </s>
<s> But in your mastering of them lies the mastery over the reader </s>
<s> This will reach you at Knebworth, I hope, to-morrow afternoon </s>
<s> Pray give your doubts to the winds of that high spot, and believe that if I had them I would swarm up the flag-staff quite as nimbly as Margrave and nail the Fenwick colours to the top </s>
<s> Ever affectionately yours </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Mrs Milner Gibson.] GAD'S HILL, _Monday, Eighth July, 1861._ MY DEAR MRS </s>
<s> GIBSON, I want very affectionately and earnestly to congratulate you on your eldest daughter's approaching marriage </s>
<s> Up to the moment when Mary told me of it, I had foolishly thought of her always as the pretty little girl with the frank loving face whom I saw last on the sands at Broadstairs </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Mr H </s>

<s> Adams.] GAD'S HILL PLACE, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, KENT, _Sunday, Sixth October, 1861._ MY DEAR MR </s>
<s> ADAMS, My readings are a sad subject to me just now, for I am going away on the 28th to read fifty times, and I have lost Mr Arthur Smith--a friend whom I can never replace--who always went with me, and transacted, as no other man ever can, all the business connected with them, and without whom, I fear, they will be dreary and weary to me </s>

<s> I desire to be useful to the Institution of the place with which my childhood is inseparably associated, and I will serve it this next Christmas if I can </s>
<s> Will you tell me when I could do you most good by reading for you </s>
<s> Faithfully yours </s>

<s> 19 and 20 </s>
<s> I have not the least doubt of the introduced matter; whether considered for its policy, its beauty, or its wise bearing on the story, it is decidedly a great improvement </s>
<s> It is at once very suggestive and very new to have these various points of view presented to the reader's mind </s>
<s> That the audience is good enough for anything that is well presented to it, I am quite sure </s>
<s> When you can avoid _notes_, however, and get their substance into the text, it is highly desirable in the case of so large an audience, simply because, as so large an audience necessarily reads the story in small portions, it is of the greater importance that they should retain as much of its argument as possible </s>
<s> Whereas the difficulty of getting numbers of people to read notes (which they invariably regard as interruptions of the text, not as strengtheners or elucidators of it) is wonderful </s>

<s> [Sidenote: The same.] GAD'S HILL PLACE, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, KENT, _Friday, Twenty-fourth January, 1862._ MY DEAR BULWER LYTTON, I have considered your questions, and here follow my replies </s>
<s> 1 </s>
<s> I think you undoubtedly _have_ the right to forbid the turning of your play into an opera </s>
<s> 2 </s>
<s> I do _not_ think the production of such an opera in the slightest degree likely to injure the play or to render it a less valuable property than it is now </s>
<s> If it could have any effect on so standard and popular a work as "The Lady of Lyons," the effect would, in my judgment, be beneficial </s>
<s> But I believe the play to be high above any such influence </s>
<s> 3 </s>
<s> Assuming you do consent to the adaptation, in a desire to oblige Oxenford, I would not recommend your asking any pecuniary compensation </s>
<s> This for two reasons: firstly, because the compensation could only be small at the best; secondly, because your taking it would associate you (unreasonably, but not the less assuredly) with the opera </s>
<s> The only objection I descry is purely one of feeling </s>
<s> Pauline trotting about in front of the float, invoking the orchestra with a limp pocket-handkerchief, is a notion that makes goose-flesh of my back </s>
<s> Also a yelping tenor going away to the wars in a scene a half-an-hour long is painful to contemplate </s>
<s> Damas, too, as a bass, with a grizzled bald head, blatently bellowing about Years long ago, When the sound of the drum First made his blood glow With a rum ti tum tum-- rather sticks in my throat; but there really seems to me to be no other objection, if you can get over this </s>
<s> Ever affectionately </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr Baylis.] GAD'S HILL PLACE, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, KENT, _Saturday, First February, 1862._ MY DEAR MR </s>
<s> BAYLIS, I have just come home </s>
<s> Finding your note, I write to you at once, or you might do me the wrong of supposing me unmindful of it and you </s>
<s> I agree with you about Smith himself, and I don't think it necessary to pursue the painful subject </s>
<s> Such things are at an end, I think, for the time being;--fell to the ground with the poor man at Cremorne </s>
<s> If they should be resumed, then they must be attacked; but I hope the fashion (far too much encouraged in its Blondin-beginning by those who should know much better) is over </s>
<s> It always appears to me that the common people have an excuse in their patronage of such exhibitions which people above them in condition have not </s>
<s> Their lives are full of physical difficulties, and they like to see such difficulties overcome </s>
<s> They go to see them overcome </s>
<s> If I am in danger of falling off a scaffold or a ladder any day, the man who claims that he can't fall from anything is a very wonderful and agreeable person to me </s>
<s> Faithfully yours always </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr Henry F </s>
<s> Chorley.] 16, HYDE PARK GATE, SOUTH KENSINGTON GORE, W., _Saturday, 1st March, 1862._ MY DEAR CHORLEY, I was at your lecture[73] this afternoon, and I hope I may venture to tell you that I was extremely pleased and interested </s>
<s> Both the matter of the materials and the manner of their arrangement were quite admirable, and a modesty and complete absence of any kind of affectation pervaded the whole discourse, which was quite an example to the many whom it concerns </s>
<s> If you could be a very little louder, and would never let a sentence go for the thousandth part of an instant until the last word is out, you would find the audience more responsive </s>
<s> A spoken sentence will never run alone in all its life, and is never to be trusted to itself in its most insignificant member </s>
<s> See it _well out_--with the voice--and the part of the audience is made surprisingly easier </s>
<s> In that excellent description of the Spanish mendicant and his guitar, as well as the very happy touches about the dance and the castanets, the people were really desirous to express very hearty appreciation; but by giving them rather too much to do in watching and listening for latter words, you stopped them </s>
<s> I take the liberty of making the remark, as one who has fought with beasts (oratorically) in divers arenas </s>
<s> For the rest nothing could be better </s>
<s> Knowledge, ingenuity, neatness, condensation, good sense, and good taste in delightful combination </s>
<s> Affectionately always </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mrs Austin.] PARIS, RUE DU FAUBOURG ST </s>
<s> HONORÉ, 27, _Friday, Seventh November, 1862._ MY DEAR LETITIA, I should have written to you from here sooner, but for having been constantly occupied </s>
<s> Your improved account of yourself is very cheering and hopeful </s>
<s> Through determined occupation and action, lies the way </s>
<s> Be sure of it </s>
<s> I came over to France before Georgina and Mary, and went to Boulogne to meet them coming in by the steamer on the great Sunday--the day of the storm </s>
<s> I stood (holding on with both hands) on the pier at Boulogne, five hours </s>
<s> The Sub-Marine Telegraph had telegraphed their boat as having come out of Folkestone--though the companion boat from Boulogne didn't try it--and at nine o'clock at night, she being due at six, there were no signs of her </s>
<s> My principal dread was, that she would try to get into Boulogne; which she could not possibly have done without carrying away everything on deck </s>
<s> The tide at nine o'clock being too low for any such desperate attempt, I thought it likely that they had run for the Downs and would knock about there all night </s>
<s> So I went to the Inn to dry my pea-jacket and get some dinner anxiously enough, when, at about ten, came a telegram from them at Calais to say they had run in there </s>
<s> To Calais I went, post, next morning, expecting to find them half-dead (of course, they had arrived half-drowned), but I found them elaborately got up to come on to Paris by the next Train, and the most wonderful thing of all was, that they hardly seem to have been frightened </s>
<s> Of course, they had discovered at the end of the voyage, that a young bride and her husband, the only other passengers on deck, and with whom they had been talking all the time, were an officer from Chatham whom they knew very well (when dry), just married and going to India </s>
<s> So they all set up house-keeping together at Dessin's at Calais (where I am well known), and looked as if they had been passing a mild summer there </s>
<s> We have a pretty apartment here, but house-rent is awful to mention </s>
<s> Mrs Bouncer (muzzled by the Parisian police) is also here, and is a wonderful spectacle to behold in the streets, restrained like a raging Lion </s>
<s> I learn from an embassy here, that the Emperor has just made an earnest proposal to our Government to unite with France (and Russia, if Russia will) in an appeal to America to stop the brutal war </s>
<s> Our Government's answer is not yet received, but I think I clearly perceive that the proposal will be declined, on the ground "that the time has not yet come" </s>
<s> Ever affectionately </s>
<s> FOOTNOTE: [73] The first of the series on "National Music" </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Mr Forster.] OFFICE OF "ALL THE YEAR ROUND," _Friday, 26th January, 1866._ MY DEAR FORSTER, I most heartily hope that your doleful apprehensions will prove unfounded </s>
<s> These changes from muggy weather to slight sharp frost, and back again, touch weak places, as I find by my own foot; but the touch goes by </s>
<s> May it prove so with you </s>
<s> Yesterday Captain ----, Captain ----, and Captain ----, dined at Gad's </s>
<s> They are, all three, naval officers of the highest reputation </s>
<s> ---- is supposed to be the best sailor in our Service </s>
<s> I said I had been remarking at home, _� propos_ of the _London_, that I knew of no shipwreck of a large strong ship (not carrying weight of guns) in the open sea, and that I could find none such in the shipwreck books </s>
<s> They all agreed that the unfortunate Captain Martin _must_ have been unacquainted with the truth as to what can and what can not be done with a Steamship having rigging and canvas; and that no sailor would dream of turning a ship's stern to such a gale--_unless his vessel could run faster than the sea_ </s>
<s> ---- said (and the other two confirmed) that the _London_ was the better for everything that she lost aloft in such a gale, and that with her head kept to the wind by means of a storm topsail--which is hoisted from the deck and requires no man to be sent aloft, and can be set under the worst circumstances--the disaster could not have occurred </s>
<s> If he had no such sail, he could have improvised it, even of hammocks and the like </s>
<s> They said that under a Board of Enquiry into the wreck, any efficient witness must of necessity state this as the fact, and could not possibly avoid the conclusion that the seamanship was utterly bad; and as to the force of the wind, for which I suggested allowance, they all had been in West Indian hurricanes and in Typhoons, and had put the heads of their ships to the wind under the most adverse circumstances </s>
<s> I thought you might be interested in this, as you have no doubt been interested in the case </s>
<s> They had a great respect for the unfortunate Captain's character, and for his behaviour when the case was hopeless, but they had not the faintest doubt that he lost the ship and those two hundred and odd lives </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Anonymous.] GAD'S HILL, _Thursday, 27th December, 1866._ DEAR MADAM,[81] You make an absurd, though common mistake, in supposing that any human creature can help you to be an authoress, if you cannot become one in virtue of your own powers </s>
<s> I know nothing about "impenetrable barrier," "outsiders," and "charmed circles" </s>
<s> I know that anyone who can write what is suitable to the requirements of my own journal--for instance--is a person I am heartily glad to discover, and do not very often find </s>
<s> And I believe this to be no rare case in periodical literature </s>
<s> I cannot undertake to advise you in the abstract, as I number my unknown correspondents by the hundred </s>
<s> But if you offer anything to me for insertion in "All the Year Round," you may be sure that it will be honestly read, and that it will be judged by no test but its own merits and adaptability to those pages </s>
<s> But I am bound to add that I do not regard successful fiction as a thing to be achieved in "leisure moments" </s>
<s> Faithfully yours </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Hon </s>
<s> Robert Lytton.] GAD'S HILL PLACE, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, KENT, _Wednesday, 17th April, 1867._ MY DEAR ROBERT LYTTON,[82] It would have been really painful to me, if I had seen you and yours at a Reading of mine in right of any other credentials than my own </s>
<s> Your appreciation has given me higher and purer gratification than your modesty can readily believe </s>
<s> When I first entered on this interpretation of myself (then quite strange in the public ear) I was sustained by the hope that I could drop into some hearts, some new expression of the meaning of my books, that would touch them in a new way </s>
<s> To this hour that purpose is so strong in me, and so real are my fictions to myself, that, after hundreds of nights, I come with a feeling of perfect freshness to that little red table, and laugh and cry with my hearers, as if I had never stood there before </s>
<s> You will know from this what a delight it is to be delicately understood, and why your earnest words cannot fail to move me </s>
<s> We are delighted to be remembered by your charming wife, and I am entrusted with more messages from this house to her, than you would care to give or withhold, so I suppress them myself and absolve you from the difficulty </s>
<s> Affectionately yours </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr Henry W </s>
<s> Phillips.] GAD'S HILL, _Thursday, 16th April, 1867._ MY DEAR MR </s>
<s> PHILLIPS,[83] Although I think the scheme has many good points, I have this doubt: Would boys so maintained at any one of our great public schools stand at a decided disadvantage towards boys not so maintained </s>
<s> Foundation Scholars, in many cases, win their way into public schools and so enforce respect and even assert superiority </s>
<s> In many other cases their patron is a remote and misty person, or Institution, sanctioned by Time and custom </s>
<s> But the proposed position would be a very different one for a student to hold, and boys are too often inconsiderate, proud, and cruel </s>
<s> I should like to know whether this point has received consideration from the projectors of the design </s>
<s> Faithfully yours always </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr Henry F </s>
<s> Chorley.] GAD'S HILL PLACE, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, KENT, _Sunday, June 2nd, 1867._ MY DEAR CHORLEY, Thank God I have come triumphantly through the heavy work of the fifty-one readings, and am wonderfully fresh </s>
<s> I grieve to hear of your sad occupation </s>
<s> You know where to find rest, and quiet, and sympathy, when you can change the dreary scene </s>
<s> I saw poor dear Stanfield (on a hint from his eldest son) in a day's interval between two expeditions </s>
<s> It was clear that the shadow of the end had fallen on him </s>
<s> It happened well that I had seen, on a wild day at Tynemouth, a remarkable sea-effect, of which I wrote a description to him, and he had kept it under his pillow </s>
<s> This place is looking very pretty </s>
<s> The freshness and repose of it, after all those thousands of gas-lighted faces, sink into the soul.[84] [Sidenote: Mr James T </s>
<s> Fields.] _September 3rd, 1867._ MY DEAR FIELDS,[85] Your cheering letter of the 21st of August arrived here this morning </s>
<s> A thousand thanks for it </s>
<s> I begin to think (nautically) that I "head west'ard" </s>
<s> You shall hear from me fully and finally as soon as Dolby shall have reported personally </s>
<s> The other day I received a letter from Mr ----, of New York (who came over in the winning yacht, and described the voyage in _The Times_), saying he would much like to see me </s>
<s> I made an appointment in London, and observed that when he _did_ see me he was obviously astonished </s>
<s> While I was sensible that the magnificence of my appearance would fully account for his being overcome, I nevertheless angled for the cause of his surprise </s>
<s> He then told me that there was a paragraph going round the papers to the effect that I was "in a critical state of health" </s>
<s> I asked him if he was sure it wasn't "cricketing" state of health </s>
<s> To which he replied, Quite </s>
<s> I then asked him down here to dinner, and he was again staggered by finding me in sporting training; also much amused </s>
<s> Yesterday's and to-day's post bring me this unaccountable paragraph from hosts of uneasy friends, with the enormous and wonderful addition that "eminent surgeons" are sending me to America for "cessation from literary labour"!! </s>
<s> So I have written a quiet line to _The Times_, certifying to my own state of health, and have also begged Dixon to do the like in _The Athenæum_ </s>
<s> I mention the matter to you, in order that you may contradict, from me, if the nonsense should reach America unaccompanied by the truth </s>
<s> But I suppose that _The New York Herald_ will probably have got the letter from Mr ---- aforesaid </s>
<s> </s>
<s> </s>
<s> </s>
<s> Charles Reade and Wilkie Collins are here; and the joke of the time is to feel my pulse when I appear at table, and also to inveigle innocent messengers to come over to the summer-house, where I write (the place is quite changed since you were here, and a tunnel under the highroad connects this shrubbery with the front garden), to ask, with their compliments, how I find myself _now_ </s>
<s> If I come to America this next November, even you can hardly imagine with what interest I shall try Copperfield on an American audience, or, if they give me their heart, how freely and fully I shall give them mine </s>
<s> We will ask Dolby then whether he ever heard it before </s>
<s> I cannot thank you enough for your invaluable help to Dolby </s>
<s> He writes that at every turn and moment the sense and knowledge and tact of Mr Osgood are inestimable to him </s>
<s> Ever, my dear Fields, faithfully yours </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Lord Lytton.] "ALL THE YEAR ROUND" OFFICE, _Tuesday, 17th September, 1867._ MY DEAR LYTTON, I am happy to tell you that the play was admirably done last night, and made a marked impression </s>
<s> Pauline is weak, but so carefully trained and fitted into the picture as to be never disagreeable, and sometimes (as in the last scene) very pathetic </s>
<s> Fechter has played nothing nearly so well as Claude since he played in Paris in the "Dame aux Camélias," or in London as Ruy Blas </s>
<s> He played the fourth act as finely as Macready, and the first much better </s>
<s> The dress and bearing in the fifth act are quite new, and quite excellent </s>
<s> Of the Scenic arrangements, the most noticeable are:--the picturesque struggle of the cottage between the taste of an artist, and the domestic means of poverty (expressed to the eye with infinite tact);--the view of Lyons (Act v </s>
<s> Scene 1), with a foreground of quay wall which the officers are leaning on, waiting for the general;--and the last scene--a suite of rooms giving on a conservatory at the back, through which the moon is shining </s>
<s> You are to understand that all these scenic appliances are subdued to the Piece, instead of the Piece being sacrificed to them; and that every group and situation has to be considered, not only with a reference to each by itself, but to the whole story </s>
<s> Beauséant's speaking the original contents of the letter was a decided point, and the immense house was quite breathless when the Tempter and the Tempted stood confronted as he made the proposal </s>
<s> There was obviously a great interest in seeing a Frenchman play the part </s>
<s> The scene between Claude and Gaspar (the small part very well done) was very closely watched for the same reason, and was loudly applauded </s>
<s> I cannot say too much of the brightness, intelligence, picturesqueness, and care of Fechter's impersonation throughout </s>
<s> There was a remarkable delicacy in his gradually drooping down on his way home with his bride, until he fell upon the table, a crushed heap of shame and remorse, while his mother told Pauline the story </s>
<s> His gradual recovery of himself as he formed better resolutions was equally well expressed; and his being at last upright again and rushing enthusiastically to join the army, brought the house down </s>
<s> I wish you could have been there </s>
<s> He never spoke English half so well as he spoke your English; and the audience heard it with the finest sympathy and respect </s>
<s> I felt that I should have been very proud indeed to have been the writer of the Play </s>
<s> Ever affectionately </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr James T </s>
<s> Fields.] [86]_October, 1867._ MY DEAR FIELDS, I hope the telegraph clerks did not mutilate out of recognition or reasonable guess the words I added to Dolby's last telegram to Boston </s>
<s> "_Tribune_ London correspondent totally false" </s>
<s> Not only is there not a word of truth in the pretended conversation, but it is so absurdly unlike me that I cannot suppose it to be even invented by anyone who ever heard me exchange a word with mortal creature </s>
<s> For twenty years I am perfectly certain that I have never made any other allusion to the republication of my books in America than the good-humoured remark, "that if there had been international copyright between England and the States, I should have been a man of very large fortune, instead of a man of moderate savings, always supporting a very expensive public position" </s>
<s> Nor have I ever been such a fool as to charge the absence of international copyright upon individuals </s>
<s> Nor have I ever been so ungenerous as to disguise or suppress the fact that I have received handsome sums for advance sheets </s>
<s> When I was in the States, I said what I had to say on the question, and there an end </s>
<s> I am absolutely certain that I have never since expressed myself, even with soreness, on the subject </s>
<s> Reverting to the preposterous fabrication of the London correspondent, the statement that I ever talked about "these fellows" who republished my books or pretended to know (what I don't know at this instant) who made how much out of them, or ever talked of their sending me "conscience money," is as grossly and completely false as the statement that I ever said anything to the effect that I could not be expected to have an interest in the American people </s>
<s> And nothing can by any possibility be falser than that </s>
<s> Again and again in these pages ("All the Year Round") I have expressed my interest in them </s>
<s> You will see it in the "Child's History of England" </s>
<s> You will see it in the last preface to "American Notes" </s>
<s> Every American who has ever spoken with me in London, Paris, or where not, knows whether I have frankly said, "You could have no better introduction to me than your country" </s>
<s> And for years and years when I have been asked about reading in America, my invariable reply has been, "I have so many friends there, and constantly receive so many earnest letters from personally unknown readers there, that, but for domestic reasons, I would go to-morrow" </s>
<s> I think I must, in the confidential intercourse between you and me, have written you to this effect more than once </s>
<s> The statement of the London correspondent from beginning to end is false </s>
<s> It is false in the letter and false in the spirit </s>
<s> He may have been misinformed, and the statement may not have originated with him </s>
<s> With whomsoever it originated, it never originated with me, and consequently is false </s>
<s> More than enough about it </s>
<s> As I hope to see you so soon, my dear Fields, and as I am busily at work on the Christmas number, I will not make this a longer letter than I can help </s>
<s> I thank you most heartily for your proffered hospitality, and need not tell you that if I went to any friend's house in America, I would go to yours </s>
<s> But the readings are very hard work, and I think I cannot do better than observe the rule on that side of the Atlantic which I observe on this, of never, under such circumstances, going to a friend's house, but always staying at a hotel </s>
<s> I am able to observe it here, by being consistent and never breaking it </s>
<s> If I am equally consistent there, I can (I hope) offend no one </s>
<s> Dolby sends his love to you and all his friends (as I do), and is girding up his loins vigorously </s>
<s> Ever, my dear Fields, Heartily and affectionately yours </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Lord Lytton.] GAD'S HILL PLACE, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, KENT, _Monday, 14th October, 1867._ MY DEAR LYTTON, I am truly delighted to find that you are so well pleased with Fechter in "The Lady of Lyons" </s>
<s> It was a labour of love with him, and I hold him in very high regard </s>
<s> _Don't_ give way to laziness, and _do_ proceed with that play </s>
<s> There never was a time when a good new play was more wanted, or had a better opening for itself </s>
<s> Fechter is a thorough artist, and what he may sometimes want in personal force is compensated by the admirable whole he can make of a play, and his perfect understanding of its presentation as a picture to the eye and mind </s>
<s> I leave London on the 8th of November early, and sail from Liverpool on the 9th </s>
<s> Ever affectionately yours </s>
<s> [Sidenote: The same.] "ALL THE YEAR ROUND" OFFICE, _Friday, 25th October, 1867._ MY DEAR LYTTON, I have read the Play[88] with great attention, interest, and admiration; and I need not say to _you_ that the art of it--the fine construction--the exquisite nicety of the touches--with which it is wrought out--have been a study to me in the pursuit of which I have had extraordinary relish </s>
<s> Taking the Play as it stands, I have nothing whatever to add to your notes and memoranda of the points to be touched again, except that I have a little uneasiness in that burst of anger and inflexibility consequent on having been deceived, coming out of Hegio </s>
<s> I see the kind of actor who _must_ play Hegio, and I see that the audience will not believe in his doing anything so serious </s>
<s> (I suppose it would be impossible to get this effect out of the mother--or through the mother's influence, instead of out of the godfather of Hegiopolis?) Now, as to the classical ground and manners of the Play </s>
<s> I suppose the objection to the Greek dress to be already--as Defoe would write it, "gotten over" by your suggestion </s>
<s> I suppose the dress not to be conventionally associated with stilts and boredom, but to be new to the public eye and very picturesque </s>
<s> Grant all that;--the names remain </s>
<s> Now, not only used such names to be inseparable in the public mind from stately weariness, but of late days they have become inseparable in the same public mind from silly puns upon the names, and from Burlesque </s>
<s> You do not know (I hope, at least, for my friend's sake) what the Strand Theatre is </s>
<s> A Greek name and a break-down nigger dance, have become inseparable there </s>
<s> I do not mean to say that your genius may not be too powerful for such associations; but I do most positively mean to say that you would lose half the play in overcoming them </s>
<s> At the best you would have to contend against them through the first three acts </s>
<s> The old tendency to become frozen on classical ground would be in the best part of the audience; the new tendency to titter on such ground would be in the worst part </s>
<s> And instead of starting fair with the audience, it is my conviction that you would start with them against you and would have to win them over </s>
<s> Furthermore, with reference to your note to me on this head, you take up a position with reference to poor dear Talfourd's "Ion" which I altogether dispute </s>
<s> It never was a popular play, I say </s>
<s> It derived a certain amount of out-of-door's popularity from the circumstances under which, and the man by whom, it was written </s>
<s> But I say that it never was a popular play on the Stage, and never made out a case of attraction there </s>
<s> As to changing the ground to Russia, let me ask you, did you ever see the "Nouvelles Russes" of Nicolas Gogol, translated into French by Louis Viardot </s>
<s> There is a story among them called "Tarass Boulla," in which, as it seems to me, all the conditions you want for such transplantation are to be found </s>
<s> So changed, you would have the popular sympathy with the Slave or Serf, or Prisoner of War, from the first </s>
<s> But I do not think it is to be got, save at great hazard, and with lamentable waste of force on the ground the Play now occupies </s>
<s> I shall keep this note until to-morrow to correct my conviction if I can see the least reason for correcting it; but I feel very confident indeed that I cannot be shaken in it </s>
<s> * * * * * _Saturday._ I have thought it over again, and have gone over the play again with an imaginary stage and actors before me, and I am still of the same mind </s>
<s> Shall I keep the MS </s>
<s> till you come to town </s>
<s> Believe me, ever affectionately yours </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr Fechter.] PARKER HOUSE, BOSTON, _3rd December, 1867._ MY DEAR FECHTER, I have been very uneasy about you, seeing in the paper that you were taken ill on the stage </s>
<s> But a letter from Georgy this morning reassures me by giving me a splendid account of your triumphant last night at the Lyceum </s>
<s> I hope to bring out our Play[89] with Wallack in New York, and to have it played in many other parts of the States </s>
<s> I have sent to Wilkie for models, etc If I waited for time to do more than write you my love, I should miss the mail to-morrow </s>
<s> Take my love, then, my dear fellow, and believe me ever Your affectionate </s>

<s> _3rd February, 1868._ [90]Articles of Agreement entered into at Baltimore, in the United States of America, this third day of February in the year of our Lord one thousand eight hundred and sixty-eight, between ---- ----, British subject, _alias_ the man of Ross, and ---- ---- ----, American citizen, _alias_ the Boston Bantam </s>
<s> Whereas, some Bounce having arisen between the above men in reference to feats of pedestrianism and agility, they have agreed to settle their differences and prove who is the better man, by means of a walking-match for two hats a side and the glory of their respective countries; and whereas they agree that the said match shall come off, whatsoever the weather, on the Mill Dam Road outside Boston, on Saturday, the twenty-ninth day of this present month; and whereas they agree that the personal attendants on themselves during the whole walk, and also the umpires and starters and declarers of victory in the match shall be ---- ---- of Boston, known in sporting circles as Massachusetts Jemmy, and Charles Dickens of Falstaff's Gad's Hill, whose surprising performances (without the least variation) on that truly national instrument, the American catarrh, have won for him the well-merited title of the Gad's Hill Gasper: 1 </s>
<s> The men are to be started, on the day appointed, by Massachusetts Jemmy and The Gasper </s>
<s> 2 </s>
<s> Jemmy and The Gasper are, on some previous day, to walk out at the rate of not less than four miles an hour by The Gasper's watch, for one hour and a half </s>
<s> At the expiration of that one hour and a half they are to carefully note the place at which they halt </s>
<s> On the match's coming off they are to station themselves in the middle of the road, at that precise point, and the men (keeping clear of them and of each other) are to turn round them, right shoulder inward, and walk back to the starting-point </s>
<s> The man declared by them to pass the starting-point first is to be the victor and the winner of the match </s>
<s> 3 </s>
<s> No jostling or fouling allowed </s>
<s> 4 </s>
<s> All cautions or orders issued to the men by the umpires, starters, and declarers of victory to be considered final and admitting of no appeal </s>
<s> A sporting narrative of the match to be written by The Gasper within one week after its coming off, and the same to be duly printed (at the expense of the subscribers to these articles) on a broadside </s>
<s> The said broadside to be framed and glazed, and one copy of the same to be carefully preserved by each of the subscribers to these articles </s>
<s> 6 </s>
<s> The men to show on the evening of the day of walking at six o'clock precisely, at the Parker House, Boston, when and where a dinner will be given them by The Gasper </s>
<s> The Gasper to occupy the chair, faced by Massachusetts Jemmy </s>
<s> The latter promptly and formally to invite, as soon as may be after the date of these presents, the following guests to honour the said dinner with their presence; that is to say [here follow the names of a few of his friends, whom he wished to be invited] </s>
<s> Now, lastly </s>
<s> In token of their accepting the trusts and offices by these articles conferred upon them, these articles are solemnly and formally signed by Massachusetts Jemmy and by the Gad's Hill Gasper, as well as by the men themselves </s>
<s> Signed by the Man of Ross, otherwise ---- </s>
<s> Signed by the Boston Bantam, otherwise ---- </s>
<s> Signed by Massachusetts Jemmy, otherwise ---- </s>
<s> Signed by the Gad's Hill Gasper, otherwise Charles Dickens </s>
<s> Witness to the signatures, ---- </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr Charles Lanman.] WASHINGTON, _February 5th, 1868._ MY DEAR SIR, Allow me to thank you most cordially for your kind letter, and for its accompanying books </s>
<s> I have a particular love for books of travel, and shall wander into the "Wilds of America" with great interest </s>
<s> I have also received your charming Sketch with great pleasure and admiration </s>
<s> Let me thank you for it heartily </s>
<s> As a beautiful suggestion of nature associated with this country, it shall have a quiet place on the walls of my house as long as I live </s>
<s> Your reference to my dear friend Washington Irving renews the vivid impressions reawakened in my mind at Baltimore the other day </s>
<s> I saw his fine face for the last time in that city </s>
<s> He came there from New York to pass a day or two with me before I went westward, and they were made among the most memorable of my life by his delightful fancy and genial humour </s>
<s> Some unknown admirer of his books and mine sent to the hotel a most enormous mint julep, wreathed with flowers </s>
<s> We sat, one on either side of it, with great solemnity (it filled a respectable-sized paper), but the solemnity was of very short duration </s>
<s> It was quite an enchanted julep, and carried us among innumerable people and places that we both knew </s>
<s> The julep held out far into the night, and my memory never saw him afterward otherwise than as bending over it, with his straw, with an attempted gravity (after some anecdote, involving some wonderfully droll and delicate observation of character), and then, as his eyes caught mine, melting into that captivating laugh of his which was the brightest and best I have ever heard </s>
<s> Dear Sir, with many thanks, faithfully yours </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mrs Pease.] BALTIMORE, _9th February, 1868._ DEAR MADAM, Mr Dolby has _not_ come between us, and I have received your letter </s>
<s> My answer to it is, unfortunately, brief </s>
<s> I am not coming to Cleveland or near it </s>
<s> Every evening on which I can possibly read during the remainder of my stay in the States is arranged for, and the fates divide me from "the big woman with two smaller ones in tow" </s>
<s> So I send her my love (to be shared in by the two smaller ones, if she approve--but not otherwise), and seriously assure her that her pleasant letter has been most welcome </s>
<s> Dear madam, faithfully your friend </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr James T </s>
<s> Fields.] ABOARD THE "RUSSIA," BOUND FOR LIVERPOOL, _Sunday, 26th April, 1868._ MY DEAR FIELDS, In order that you may have the earliest intelligence of me, I begin this note to-day in my small cabin, purposing (if it should prove practicable) to post it at Queenstown for the return steamer </s>
<s> We are already past the Banks of Newfoundland, although our course was seventy miles to the south, with the view of avoiding ice seen by Judkins in the _Scotia_ on his passage out to New York </s>
<s> The _Russia_ is a magnificent ship, and has dashed along bravely </s>
<s> We had made more than thirteen hundred and odd miles at noon to-day </s>
<s> The wind, after being a little capricious, rather threatens at the present time to turn against us, but our run is already eighty miles ahead of the _Russia's_ last run in this direction--a very fast one </s>
<s> </s>
<s> </s>
<s> </s>
<s> To all whom it may concern, report the _Russia_ in the highest terms </s>
<s> She rolls more easily than the other Cunard Screws, is kept in perfect order, and is most carefully looked after in all departments </s>
<s> We have had nothing approaching to heavy weather, still one can speak to the trim of the ship </s>
<s> Her captain, a gentleman; bright, polite, good-natured, and vigilant </s>
<s> </s>
<s> </s>
<s> </s>
<s> As to me, I am greatly better, I hope </s>
<s> I have got on my right boot to-day for the first time; the "true American" seems to be turning faithless at last; and I made a Gad's Hill breakfast this morning, as a further advance on having otherwise eaten and drunk all day ever since Wednesday </s>
<s> You will see Anthony Trollope, I daresay </s>
<s> What was my amazement to see him with these eyes come aboard in the mail tender just before we started </s>
<s> He had come out in the _Scotia_ just in time to dash off again in said tender to shake hands with me, knowing me to be aboard here </s>
<s> It was most heartily done </s>
<s> He is on a special mission of convention with the United States post-office </s>
<s> We have been picturing your movements, and have duly checked off your journey home, and have talked about you continually </s>
<s> But I have thought about you both, even much, much more </s>
<s> You will never know how I love you both; or what you have been to me in America, and will always be to me everywhere; or how fervently I thank you </s>
<s> All the working of the ship seems to be done on my forehead </s>
<s> It is scrubbed and holystoned (my head--not the deck) at three every morning </s>
<s> It is scraped and swabbed all day </s>
<s> Eight pairs of heavy boots are now clattering on it, getting the ship under sail again </s>
<s> Legions of ropes'-ends are flopped upon it as I write, and I must leave off with Dolby's love </s>
<s> * * * * * _Thursday, 30th._ Soon after I left off as above we had a gale of wind which blew all night </s>
<s> For a few hours on the evening side of midnight there was no getting from this cabin of mine to the saloon, or _vice versâ_, so heavily did the sea break over the decks </s>
<s> The ship, however, made nothing of it, and we were all right again by Monday afternoon </s>
<s> Except for a few hours yesterday (when we had a very light head-wind), the weather has been constantly favourable, and we are now bowling away at a great rate, with a fresh breeze filling all our sails </s>
<s> We expect to be at Queenstown between midnight and three in the morning </s>
<s> I hope, my dear Fields, you may find this legible, but I rather doubt it, for there is motion enough on the ship to render writing to a landsman, however accustomed to pen and ink, rather a difficult achievement </s>

<s> Fields.] GAD'S HILL, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, KENT, _25th May, 1868._ MY DEAR MRS </s>
<s> FIELDS, As you ask me about the dogs, I begin with them </s>
<s> When I came down first, I came to Gravesend, five miles off </s>
<s> The two Newfoundland dogs, coming to meet me with the usual carriage and the usual driver, and beholding me coming in my usual dress out at the usual door, it struck me that their recollection of my having been absent for any unusual time was at once cancelled </s>
<s> They behaved (they are both young dogs) exactly in their usual manner; coming behind the basket phaeton as we trotted along, and lifting their heads to have their ears pulled--a special attention which they receive from no one else </s>
<s> But when I drove into the stable-yard, Linda (the St </s>
<s> Bernard) was greatly excited; weeping profusely, and throwing herself on her back that she might caress my foot with her great fore-paws </s>
<s> Mamie's little dog, too, Mrs Bouncer, barked in the greatest agitation on being called down and asked by Mamie, "Who is this" </s>
<s> and tore round and round me, like the dog in the Faust outlines </s>
<s> You must know that all the farmers turned out on the road in their market-chaises to say, "Welcome home, sir" </s>
<s> and that all the houses along the road were dressed with flags; and that our servants, to cut out the rest, had dressed this house so that every brick of it was hidden </s>
<s> They had asked Mamie's permission to "ring the alarm-bell" (!) when master drove up, but Mamie, having some slight idea that that compliment might awaken master's sense of the ludicrous, had recommended bell abstinence </s>
<s> But on Sunday the village choir (which includes the bell-ringers) made amends </s>
<s> After some unusually brief pious reflections in the crowns of their hats at the end of the sermon, the ringers bolted out, and rang like mad until I got home </s>
<s> There had been a conspiracy among the villagers to take the horse out, if I had come to our own station, and draw me here </s>
<s> Mamie and Georgy had got wind of it and warned me </s>
<s> Divers birds sing here all day, and the nightingales all night </s>
<s> The place is lovely, and in perfect order </s>
<s> I have put five mirrors in the Swiss châlet (where I write) and they reflect and refract in all kinds of ways the leaves that are quivering at the windows, and the great fields of waving corn, and the sail-dotted river </s>
<s> My room is up among the branches of the trees; and the birds and the butterflies fly in and out, and the green branches shoot in, at the open windows, and the lights and shadows of the clouds come and go with the rest of the company </s>
<s> The scent of the flowers, and indeed of everything that is growing for miles and miles, is most delicious </s>
<s> Dolby (who sends a world of messages) found his wife much better than he expected, and the children (wonderful to relate!) perfect </s>
<s> The little girl winds up her prayers every night with a special commendation to Heaven of me and the pony--as if I must mount him to get there </s>
<s> I dine with Dolby (I was going to write "him," but found it would look as if I were going to dine with the pony) at Greenwich this very day, and if your ears do not burn from six to nine this evening, then the Atlantic is a non-conductor </s>
<s> We are already settling--think of this!--the details of my farewell course of readings </s>
<s> I am brown beyond belief, and cause the greatest disappointment in all quarters by looking so well </s>
<s> It is really wonderful what those fine days at sea did for me </s>
<s> My doctor was quite broken down in spirits when he saw me, for the first time since my return, last Saturday </s>
<s> "Good Lord" </s>
<s> he said, recoiling, "seven years younger" </s>
<s> It is time I should explain the otherwise inexplicable enclosure </s>
<s> Will you tell Fields, with my love (I suppose he hasn't used _all_ the pens yet?), that I think there is in Tremont Street a set of my books, sent out by Chapman, not arrived when I departed </s>
<s> Such set of the immortal works of our illustrious, etc, is designed for the gentleman to whom the enclosure is addressed </s>
<s> If T., F </s>
<s> and Co., will kindly forward the set (carriage paid) with the enclosure to ----'s address, I will invoke new blessings on their heads, and will get Dolby's little daughter to mention them nightly </s>
<s> "No Thoroughfare" is very shortly coming out in Paris, where it is now in active rehearsal </s>
<s> It is still playing here, but without Fechter, who has been very ill </s>
<s> The doctor's dismissal of him to Paris, however, and his getting better there, enables him to get up the play there </s>
<s> He and Wilkie missed so many pieces of stage-effect here, that, unless I am quite satisfied with his report, I shall go over and try my stage-managerial hand at the Vaudeville Theatre </s>
<s> I particularly want the drugging and attempted robbing in the bedroom scene at the Swiss inn to be done to the sound of a waterfall rising and falling with the wind </s>
<s> Although in the very opening of that scene they speak of the waterfall and listen to it, nobody thought of its mysterious music </s>
<s> I could make it, with a good stage-carpenter, in an hour </s>
<s> My dear love to Fields once again </s>
<s> Same to you and him from Mamie and Georgy </s>
<s> I cannot tell you both how I miss you, or how overjoyed I should be to see you here </s>
<s> Ever, my dear Mrs Fields, Your most affectionate friend </s>

<s> When he was in London the first time he came and went without reporting himself, and left me in a state of unspeakable discomfiture </s>

<s> He, the girls, and Appleton, came down last Saturday night and stayed until Monday forenoon </s>
<s> I showed them all the neighbouring country that could be shown in so short a time, and they finished off with a tour of inspection of the kitchens, pantry, wine-cellar, pickles, sauces, servants' sitting-room, general household stores, and even the Cellar Book, of this illustrious establishment </s>
<s> Forster and Kent (the latter wrote certain verses to Longfellow, which have been published in _The Times_, and which I sent to D----) came down for a day, and I hope we all had a really "good time" </s>
<s> I turned out a couple of postillions in the old red jacket of the old red royal Dover Road, for our ride; and it was like a holiday ride in England fifty years ago </s>
